		$(document).ready(function() {

    		$('.nav-links-main').clone().removeClass('nav-links nav-links-main').addClass('nav-links-clone nav-links-clone-main').prependTo('nav.nav-links-clone-wrapper');
    		$('.nav-links-tertiary .tertiary').clone().removeClass('nav-links nav-links-tertiary').addClass('nav-links-clone').appendTo('.nav-links-clone');
    		$('html').click(function() {
				$('.nav-links-clone-wrapper, .more-tertiary-links').slideUp();
				$('.nav-links-toggle, .tertiary-more-toggle').removeClass('active').attr('aria-expanded', 'false');
				$('.tertiary-more').removeClass('active');
			});
			$('.nav-links-toggle, .tertiary-more-toggle').click(function(event){
				event.stopPropagation();
			});
	    	$('.nav-links-toggle').click(function() {
	    		if($('.nav-links-clone-wrapper').is(':hidden')) {
	    			$('.nav-links-clone-wrapper').slideDown();
	    			$('.nav-links-toggle').addClass('active').attr('aria-expanded', 'true');
	    		} else {
	    			$('.nav-links-clone-wrapper').slideUp();
	    			$('.nav-links-toggle').removeClass('active').attr('aria-expanded', 'false');
	    		}
	    	});
	    	$('.tertiary-more-toggle').click(function() {
	    		if ($('.more-tertiary-links').is(':visible')) {
	    			$('.more-tertiary-links').slideUp();
	    			$('.tertiary-more').removeClass('active');
	    			$('.tertiary-more-toggle').removeClass('active').attr('aria-expanded', 'false');
	    		} else {
	    			$('.more-tertiary-links').slideDown();
	    			$('.tertiary-more').addClass('active');
	    			$('.tertiary-more-toggle').addClass('active').attr('aria-expanded', 'true');
	    		}
	    	});
	    	$(window).on("load resize scroll",function(e){
	    		$('.nav-links-clone-wrapper').hide();
				$('.nav-links-toggle, .tertiary-more-toggle').removeClass('active').attr('aria-expanded', 'false');
				$('.tertiary-more').removeClass('active');
				$('.more-tertiary-links').slideUp();
	    	});
		    $('.h_account').tooltip();
		});
	</script>

<div style="text-align:center"><span class="lbexLegisNum">H. R. 3933</span></div>
<p></p>
<br><p style="text-align:left;margin-left: 2em;" class="lbexHang">To amend the Internal Revenue Code of 1986 to prevent the
		  avoidance of tax on income from assets held abroad, and for other
		  purposes.</p>
<hr style="width:40%">
<p></p>
<div style="text-align:center"><span class="lbexChamber">IN THE HOUSE OF REPRESENTATIVES</span></div>
<div style="text-align:center">
<p></p>
<span class="lbexSimplecap">October 27, 2009</span><p></p>
</div>
<div style="text-align:left;" class="lbexHang"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHangSmalllWithMargin">Mr. <span class="lbexSimplecap"> Rangel</span> (for
			 himself, Mr. <span class="lbexSimplecap"> Neal </span>of Massachusetts,
			 Mr. <span class="lbexSimplecap"> Stark</span>,
			 Mr. <span class="lbexSimplecap"> Levin</span>,
			 Mr. <span class="lbexSimplecap"> Van Hollen</span>,
			 Mr. <span class="lbexSimplecap"> Meek </span>of Florida,
			 Mr. <span class="lbexSimplecap"> Davis </span>of Illinois, and
			 Ms. <span class="lbexSimplecap"> Linda T. Snchez </span>of California)
			 introduced the following bill; which was referred to the
			 Committee on Ways and
			 Means</p></div>
<p></p>
<hr style="width:40%">
<p></p>
<div style="text-align:center"><b><span class="lbexLegisType">A BILL</span></b></div>
<p></p>
<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHangWithMargin">To amend the Internal Revenue Code of 1986 to prevent the
		  avoidance of tax on income from assets held abroad, and for other
		  purposes.</p>
<p></p>
<div style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">
<em> Be it enacted by the Senate and House of Representatives of the
		United States of America in Congress assembled, </em><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHang"><a href="#HCB3DC7685EAD41359AE47D42D84AA94A" id="toc-HCB3DC7685EAD41359AE47D42D84AA94A"><div class="lbexHangWithMargin">
<span class="lbexSectionlevelOLC"><a id="HCB3DC7685EAD41359AE47D42D84AA94A"></a>SECTION 1.</span> <span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"> <span class="lbexAllcap">Short title, etc</span>.</span>
</div></a></p>
<a id="H895D6C4A668B489C9B17CB8F24A458D9"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(a) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Short
			 title</span>.This Act may be cited
			 as the Foreign Account Tax Compliance
			 Act of 2009.</p>
<a id="H30743BE59BEB42C5AFC4288C0DDBAF02"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(b) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Reference</span>.Except as otherwise expressly provided,
			 whenever in this Act an amendment or repeal is expressed in terms of an
			 amendment to, or repeal of, a section or other provision, the reference shall
			 be considered to be made to a section or other provision of the Internal
			 Revenue Code of 1986.</p>
<a id="H23746E628BCB4F55B5FBE4C6C12D8C1A"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(c) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Table of
			 contents</span>.The table of contents for this Act is as follows:<p></p><span><span class="lbexTocSectionOLC"><br><a href="#toc-HCB3DC7685EAD41359AE47D42D84AA94A" id="HCB3DC7685EAD41359AE47D42D84AA94A">Sec.1.Short title, etc.</a></span></span><span><div style="text-align:center" class="lbexTocDivisionOLC">
<p></p>
<a href="#toc-HCFD74AE8644A448BAA90866F04D1C018" id="HCFD74AE8644A448BAA90866F04D1C018">TITLE IINCREASED DISCLOSURE OF BENEFICIAL OWNERS <p></p></a>
</div></span><span><span class="lbexTocSectionOLC"><br><a href="#toc-HED45400FFB264706A51497DDC837473D" id="HED45400FFB264706A51497DDC837473D">Sec.101.Reporting on certain foreign accounts.</a></span></span><span><span class="lbexTocSectionOLC"><br><a href="#toc-HE5673CA625674203A24B258454BDA261" id="HE5673CA625674203A24B258454BDA261">Sec.102.Repeal of certain foreign exceptions to registered
				bond requirements.</a></span></span><span><div style="text-align:center" class="lbexTocDivisionOLC">
<p></p>
<a href="#toc-H8E0966FB328A42988C8349F497B74778" id="H8E0966FB328A42988C8349F497B74778">TITLE IIUNDER REPORTING WITH RESPECT TO FOREIGN
				ASSETS<p></p></a>
</div></span><span><span class="lbexTocSectionOLC"><br><a href="#toc-HBD3B64DF74D84602B03F4B94C3CE9BAA" id="HBD3B64DF74D84602B03F4B94C3CE9BAA">Sec.201.Disclosure of information with respect to foreign
				financial assets.</a></span></span><span><span class="lbexTocSectionOLC"><br><a href="#toc-H0B0EDC14BFE54979A3EFC5B5CF193E50" id="H0B0EDC14BFE54979A3EFC5B5CF193E50">Sec.202.Penalties for underpayments attributable to
				undisclosed foreign financial assets.</a></span></span><span><span class="lbexTocSectionOLC"><br><a href="#toc-H07FB069A9B57400390231943EA7D5887" id="H07FB069A9B57400390231943EA7D5887">Sec.203.Modification of statute of limitations for
				significant omission of income in connection with foreign assets.</a></span></span><span><div style="text-align:center" class="lbexTocDivisionOLC">
<p></p>
<a href="#toc-H5262DD62C5334F18AFEE8FFDF8AC2FC0" id="H5262DD62C5334F18AFEE8FFDF8AC2FC0">TITLE IIIOTHER DISCLOSURE PROVISIONS <p></p></a>
</div></span><span><span class="lbexTocSectionOLC"><br><a href="#toc-HB0DA248DE26C4EA193C806B397645253" id="HB0DA248DE26C4EA193C806B397645253">Sec.301.Disclosure of assistance in acquiring or forming a
				foreign entity.</a></span></span><span><span class="lbexTocSectionOLC"><br><a href="#toc-H9A7F25C14C1A43E0A3261D2FC5BF4A80" id="H9A7F25C14C1A43E0A3261D2FC5BF4A80">Sec.302.Reporting of activities with respect to passive
				foreign investment companies.</a></span></span><span><span class="lbexTocSectionOLC"><br><a href="#toc-HD548513EBE1D4CDCB6AE1D1D93CEFF12" id="HD548513EBE1D4CDCB6AE1D1D93CEFF12">Sec.303.Secretary permitted to require financial institutions
				to file certain returns related to withholding on foreign transfers
				electronically.</a></span></span><span><div style="text-align:center" class="lbexTocDivisionOLC">
<p></p>
<a href="#toc-HB3AE27AA570546AEBC7E4C8D7338FF20" id="HB3AE27AA570546AEBC7E4C8D7338FF20">TITLE IVPROVISIONS RELATED TO FOREIGN TRUSTS<p></p></a>
</div></span><span><span class="lbexTocSectionOLC"><br><a href="#toc-H15710B5859AB435CBAED79ABB9DCAFC3" id="H15710B5859AB435CBAED79ABB9DCAFC3">Sec.401.Clarifications with respect to foreign trusts which
				are treated as having a United States beneficiary.</a></span></span><span><span class="lbexTocSectionOLC"><br><a href="#toc-H1161210BDFB84F4EA0B6200CBE6D5D20" id="H1161210BDFB84F4EA0B6200CBE6D5D20">Sec.402.Presumption that foreign trust has United States
				beneficiary.</a></span></span><span><span class="lbexTocSectionOLC"><br><a href="#toc-H2490B08235284E958F8696E93813B1E0" id="H2490B08235284E958F8696E93813B1E0">Sec.403.Uncompensated use of trust property treated as a
				distribution.</a></span></span><span><span class="lbexTocSectionOLC"><br><a href="#toc-HFD65816F0A1B4C46AC8E07CDEB2267C8" id="HFD65816F0A1B4C46AC8E07CDEB2267C8">Sec.404.Reporting requirement of United States owners of
				foreign trusts.</a></span></span><span><span class="lbexTocSectionOLC"><br><a href="#toc-H9D351F98A5024AFDACBF5E39E7D6133B" id="H9D351F98A5024AFDACBF5E39E7D6133B">Sec.405.Minimum penalty with respect to failure to report on
				certain foreign trusts.</a></span></span><span><div style="text-align:center" class="lbexTocDivisionOLC">
<p></p>
<a href="#toc-H6AE826263F084DAB86EE701AE06EA42B" id="H6AE826263F084DAB86EE701AE06EA42B">TITLE VDIVIDEND EQUIVALENT PAYMENTS RECEIVED BY FOREIGN PERSONS
				TREATED AS DIVIDENDS<p></p></a>
</div></span><span><span class="lbexTocSectionOLC"><br><a href="#toc-H464E12F1029A4E1385170C9507A3F5BF" id="H464E12F1029A4E1385170C9507A3F5BF">Sec.501.Dividend equivalent payments received by foreign
				persons treated as dividends.</a></span></span></p>
<a id="HCFD74AE8644A448BAA90866F04D1C018"></a><p><div style="text-align:center"><a href="#HCFD74AE8644A448BAA90866F04D1C018" id="toc-HCFD74AE8644A448BAA90866F04D1C018"><span class="lbexTitleLevelOLC">TITLE I</span><span class="lbexTitleLevelOLC"><span style="text-align:center"></span><span class="lbexAllcap">Increased
			 disclosure of beneficial owners </span></span></a></div></p>
<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHang"><a href="#HED45400FFB264706A51497DDC837473D" id="toc-HED45400FFB264706A51497DDC837473D"><div class="lbexHangWithMargin">
<span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"><a id="HED45400FFB264706A51497DDC837473D"></a>SEC. 101. </span><span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"> <span class="lbexAllcap">Reporting on
			 certain foreign accounts</span>.</span>
</div></a></p>
<a id="H9562342B249B4298BE27E2748105EFF2"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(a) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">In
			 general</span>.The Internal Revenue
			 Code of 1986 is amended by inserting after chapter 3 the following new
			 chapter:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent"><a id="H7800A27C871C47D79A1BD24909A92FBF"></a><p></p><a id="H7800A27C871C47D79A1BD24909A92FBF"></a><p><div style="text-align:center"><a href="#H7800A27C871C47D79A1BD24909A92FBF" id="toc-H7800A27C871C47D79A1BD24909A92FBF"><span class="lbexChapterLevelOLC">CHAPTER 4</span><span class="lbexChapterLevelOLC"><span style="text-align:center"></span>TAXES TO ENFORCE
				REPORTING ON CERTAIN FOREIGN ACCOUNTS</span></a></div></p><p></p><span><span class="lbexTocSectionOLC"><br><a href="#toc-HFAFD4B2D38874D0E809825C71334742B" id="HFAFD4B2D38874D0E809825C71334742B">Sec.1471.Withholdable payments to foreign financial
				  institutions.</a></span></span><span><span class="lbexTocSectionOLC"><br><a href="#toc-H6589F36362E04CF9BED1BF6DF991DBFA" id="H6589F36362E04CF9BED1BF6DF991DBFA">Sec.1472.Withholdable payments to other foreign
				  entities.</a></span></span><span><span class="lbexTocSectionOLC"><br><a href="#toc-H46552F08BBF2450899792A9B2FB4C79D" id="H46552F08BBF2450899792A9B2FB4C79D">Sec.1473.Definitions.</a></span></span><span><span class="lbexTocSectionOLC"><br><a href="#toc-H60F8DF697564429EA8D8E0D8CB411CD6" id="H60F8DF697564429EA8D8E0D8CB411CD6">Sec.1474.Special rules.</a></span></span><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHang"><a href="#HFAFD4B2D38874D0E809825C71334742B" id="toc-HFAFD4B2D38874D0E809825C71334742B"><div class="lbexHangWithMargin">
<span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"><a id="HFAFD4B2D38874D0E809825C71334742B"></a>SEC. 1471. </span><span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"> <span class="lbexAllcap">Withholdable
				payments to foreign financial institutions</span>.</span>
</div></a></p><a id="H107C772A960D4D5C8748B36964D71C18"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(a) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">In
				general</span>.In the case of any
				withholdable payment to a foreign financial institution which does not meet the
				requirements of subsection (b), the withholding agent with respect to such
				payment shall deduct and withhold from such payment a tax equal to 30 percent
				of the amount of such payment.</p></p><a id="HEBA77940A873463BB8CAAAC3C9912632"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(b) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Reporting
				requirements, etc</span>.<a id="HEA7EF408087F470F882F92325DCC1047"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">I</span><span class="lbexSmallText">N
				GENERAL</span>.The requirements of this subsection are met with respect
				to any foreign financial institution if an agreement is in effect between such
				institution and the Secretary under which such institution agrees<a id="H32C13D23856646F093618231B8E427C2"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) to obtain such
				information from each holder of each account maintained by such institution as
				is necessary to determine which (if any) of such accounts are United States
				accounts,</p></p><a id="H6D4EC2C713224480914188536A69FCDD"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) to comply with
				such verification and due diligence procedures as the Secretary may require
				with respect to the identification of United States accounts,</p></p><a id="H996495B612E0429FBB22801638565898"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(C) in the case of any
				United States account maintained by such institution, to report on an annual
				basis (at such time and in such manner as the Secretary may provide) the
				information described in subsection (c) with respect to such account,</p></p><a id="HD6D524830109412B86A2EC22A6106CE1"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(D) to comply with
				requests by the Secretary for additional information with respect to any United
				States account maintained by such institution, and</p></p><a id="H907EDD903E4B415687BB86FC69BA7904"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(E) in any case in
				which any foreign law would (but for a waiver described in clause (i)) prevent
				the reporting of any information referred to in this subsection or subsection
				(c) with respect to any United States account maintained by such
				institution<a id="H45B73FD1A6854378B1CC1AFE77B0C754"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(i) to
				attempt to obtain a valid and effective waiver of such law from each holder of
				such account, and</p></p><a id="H2DF1DDA84B74466EAD58A594C151DC3D"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(ii) if a waiver
				described in clause (i) is not obtained from each such holder, to close such
				account.</p></p></p></p></p></p><a id="H4D1DA300C7814136B97B3FCBE9EEE5C0"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">T</span><span class="lbexSmallText">ERMINATION OF
				AGREEMENT</span>.Any agreement entered into under this subsection may be
				terminated by the Secretary upon a determination by the Secretary that the
				foreign financial institution is out of compliance with such agreement.</p></p></p></p><a id="H70A07EEBFA1C42B0A080840CF79CE1A4"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(c) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Information
				required To be reported on United States accounts</span>.<a id="H59C73D0165CE438F914C9EA94D84D292"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">I</span><span class="lbexSmallText">N
				GENERAL</span>.The agreement described in subsection (b) shall require
				the foreign financial institution to report the following with respect to each
				United States account maintained by such institution:<a id="HF55DB030B7A64F59B3A94270DB032DC2"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) The name, address,
				and TIN of each account holder which is a specified United States person and,
				in the case of any account holder which is a United States owned foreign
				entity, the name, address, and TIN of each substantial United States owner of
				such entity.</p></p><a id="HCCA636C3C27F4F0B9F72B645A1E27764"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) The account
				number.</p></p><a id="HFCFAB335ADC44EA2837065B44F891296"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(C) The account
				balance or value (determined at such time and in such manner as the Secretary
				may provide).</p></p><a id="HB008E27147EB427687D38495B73381B7"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(D) The gross receipts
				and gross withdrawals or payments from the account (determined for such period
				and in such manner as the Secretary may provide).</p></p></p></p><a id="HBBF2F1534AAA4A6D9F956BCC63DCA281"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">E</span><span class="lbexSmallText">LECTION TO BE
				SUBJECT TO SAME REPORTING AS UNITED STATES FINANCIAL
				INSTITUTIONS</span>.In the case of a foreign financial institution which
				elects the application of this paragraph<a id="H49B3649B5DC145269154EE972A9C3770"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) subparagraphs (C)
				and (D) of paragraph (1) shall not apply, and</p></p><a id="H3D5DD5ADF5404FA9845069469EE9583E"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) the agreement
				described in subsection (b) shall require such foreign financial institution to
				report such information with respect to each United States account maintained
				by such institution as such institution would be required to report under
				sections 6041, 6042, 6045, and 6049 if<a id="HC3F3C2028FE341ABBD02F7E90A288378"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(i) such institution
				were a United States person, and</p></p><a id="HE3E3A23230E34E6C86384CCDE624E785"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(ii) each holder of
				such account which is a specified United States person or United States owned
				foreign entity were a natural person and citizen of the United States.</p></p><p class="nolbexIndentSubpar">An
				election under this paragraph shall be made at such time, in such manner, and
				subject to such conditions as the Secretary may provide.</p></p></p></p></p><a id="HC81B8780061641C281075A12969509C9"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(3) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">I</span><span class="lbexSmallText">NFORMATION
				SUPPLIED BY ACCOUNT HOLDERS</span>.The foreign financial institution may rely
				on a certification from an account holder as to whether an account is a United
				States account and for the information required under paragraph (1)(A) with
				respect to such account holder if neither the financial institution nor any
				entity which is a member of the same expanded affiliated group as such
				financial institution knows, or has reason to know, that any information
				provided in such certification is incorrect.</p></p><a id="H8719AB4D1AFB48268AB54E0961BEA318"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(4) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">S</span><span class="lbexSmallText">EPARATE
				REQUIREMENTS FOR QUALIFIED INTERMEDIARIES</span>.In the case of a
				foreign financial institution which is treated as a qualified intermediary by
				the Secretary for purposes of section 1441 and the regulations issued
				thereunder, the requirements of this section shall be in addition to any
				reporting or other requirements imposed by the Secretary for purposes of such
				treatment.</p></p></p></p><a id="HD3F023636EFC4A1A89B302C1DC5C53CB"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(d) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Definitions</span>.For
				purposes of this section<a id="H44905BACC4434E998637DD35796F7E42"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">U</span><span class="lbexSmallText">NITED STATES
				ACCOUNT</span>.<a id="H79161A5224B140DF9F33F72E35FB655C"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">I</span><span class="lbexSmallText">N
				GENERAL</span>.The term United States account means any
				financial account which is held by one or more specified United States persons
				or United States owned foreign entities.</p></p><a id="HF2BDC6E0131345D28EA25879578A47B3"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">E</span><span class="lbexSmallText">XCEPTION FOR
				CERTAIN ACCOUNTS HELD BY INDIVIDUALS</span>.Unless the foreign financial institution
				elects to not have this subparagraph apply, such term shall not include any
				depository account maintained by such financial institution if<a id="HF75AFA629B2C4B59B6D6164D24CA827F"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(i) each holder of
				such account is a natural person, and</p></p><a id="H883CAC0DA5B742FD8CE97C7B7BE67ED3"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(ii) with respect to
				each holder of such account, the aggregate value of all depository accounts
				held (in whole or in part) by such holder and maintained by the same financial
				institution which maintains such account does not exceed $10,000 ($50,000 if
				all such accounts were in existence on the date of the enactment of this
				section).</p></p><p class="nolbexIndentSubpar">For
				purposes of clause (ii), all financial institutions which are members of the
				same expanded affiliated group shall be treated as a single financial
				institution.</p></p></p></p></p><a id="H41BF43CD9D414669A4B479C9F82663C6"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">F</span><span class="lbexSmallText">INANCIAL
				ACCOUNT</span>.The term
				financial account means, with respect to any financial
				institution<a id="H0DA0040D7E1E472997E50A7145D820FB"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) any depository
				account maintained by such financial institution,</p></p><a id="H20817948A47F4B81B2F59B73E460DB74"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) any custodial
				account maintained by such financial institution, and</p></p><a id="HDD048196C96745F295DB57A9662A1C3D"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(C) except as
				otherwise provided by the Secretary, any equity or debt interest in such
				financial institution (other than interests which are regularly traded on an
				established securities market).</p></p><p class="nolbexIndentParagraph">Any equity
				or debt interest which constitutes a financial account under subparagraph (C)
				with respect to any financial institution shall be treated for purposes of this
				section as maintained by such financial institution.</p></p></p><a id="HA26D0539AA2F457C98A54364A929C95E"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(3) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">U</span><span class="lbexSmallText">NITED STATES
				OWNED FOREIGN ENTITY</span>.The term United States owned foreign
				entity means any foreign entity which has one or more substantial
				United States owners.</p></p><a id="HAB7A68D0973D4D0E843387279E317501"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(4) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">F</span><span class="lbexSmallText">OREIGN
				FINANCIAL INSTITUTION</span>.The term foreign financial
				institution means any financial institution which is a foreign
				entity.</p></p><a id="H299D1BC1B89A4296B44A8DE123188226"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(5) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">F</span><span class="lbexSmallText">INANCIAL
				INSTITUTION</span>.Except as
				otherwise provided by the Secretary, the term financial
				institution means any entity that<a id="HF83F8579030B47FD9F9F346FFFEA6AFC"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) accepts deposits
				in the ordinary course of a banking or similar business,</p></p><a id="H19F269311256484AAE5EF03802F5B824"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) is engaged in the
				business of holding financial assets for the account of others, or</p></p><a id="H392019319C0A477593AC5D1538AACA8C"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(C) is engaged (or
				holding itself out as being engaged) primarily in the business of investing,
				reinvesting, or trading in securities (as defined in section 475(c)(2) without
				regard to the last sentence thereof), partnership interests, commodities (as
				defined in section 475(e)(2)), or any interest (including a futures or forward
				contract or option) in such securities, partnership interests, or
				commodities.</p></p></p></p></p></p><a id="HA1B51E7DD0F7408CBCDFC6110878CF93"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(e) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Affiliated
				groups</span>.<a id="HFC5D07E6FDE245C9847E2A9E3F61BBE8"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">I</span><span class="lbexSmallText">N
				GENERAL</span>.The requirements of subsections (b), (c)(1), and (c)(3)
				shall apply<a id="H65C2F97273F646ED9AA12E6CB0BFC92E"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) with respect to
				United States accounts maintained by the foreign financial institution,
				and</p></p><a id="H1A58AF1BF0554DB18A5DBBA38249D173"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) except as
				otherwise provided by the Secretary, with respect to United States accounts
				maintained by each other foreign financial institution (other than any foreign
				financial institution which meets the requirements of subsection (b)) which is
				a member of the same expanded affiliated group as such foreign financial
				institution.</p></p></p></p><a id="H9C067B257C2B41C9A53045A61F334D3E"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">E</span><span class="lbexSmallText">XPANDED
				AFFILIATED GROUP</span>.For purposes
				of this section, the term expanded affiliated group means an
				affiliated group as defined in section 1504(a), determined<a id="H6F3AB4156EE241889B3B997B744411BB"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) by substituting
				more than 50 percent for at least 80 percent each
				place it appears, and</p></p><a id="HAC64B2F7595C4AA4A99BE13840D1E868"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) without regard to
				paragraphs (2) and (3) of section 1504(b).</p></p><p class="nolbexIndentParagraph">A
				partnership or any other entity (other than a corporation) shall be treated as
				a member of an expanded affiliated group if such entity is controlled (within
				the meaning of section 954(d)(3)) by members of such group (including any
				entity treated as a member of such group by reason of this sentence).</p></p></p></p></p><a id="H24297B26DA064DB6ACB78476E44320AD"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(f) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Exception for
				certain payments</span>.Subsection (a) shall not apply to any payment if
				the beneficial owner of such payment is<a id="HAA2D7A3FB3E44D00BADC679FD63AC9D5"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) any foreign government, any political
				subdivision of a foreign government, or any wholly owned agency or
				instrumentality of any one or more of the foregoing,</p></p><a id="HF361C683BD084FBE9E054C7A387153C6"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) any international
				organization or any wholly owned agency or instrumentality thereof,</p></p><a id="H17826E7C951F4D4E91C66B38D99182AD"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(3) any foreign
				central bank of issue, or</p></p><a id="H1F14CF64DE824E65BD4E44C7BCC9BC1D"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(4) any other class of
				persons identified by the Secretary for purposes of this subsection as posing a
				low risk of tax evasion.</p></p></p></p><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHang"><a href="#H6589F36362E04CF9BED1BF6DF991DBFA" id="toc-H6589F36362E04CF9BED1BF6DF991DBFA"><div class="lbexHangWithMargin">
<span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"><a id="H6589F36362E04CF9BED1BF6DF991DBFA"></a>SEC. 1472. </span><span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"> <span class="lbexAllcap">Withholdable
				payments to other foreign entities</span>.</span>
</div></a></p><a id="H2A3A7DA884F44F72B7F4988DEF976381"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(a) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">In
				general</span>.In the case of any
				withholdable payment to a non-financial foreign entity, if<a id="H419EA5BAB7174B139907191F8B1D12CA"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) the beneficial
				owner of such payment is such entity or any other non-financial foreign entity,
				and</p></p><a id="HAE137844FC3B4A2895128209ECEC13EB"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) the requirements
				of subsection (b) are not met with respect to such beneficial owner,</p></p><p></p><span class="lbexNonIndentSubsection">then the
				withholding agent with respect to such payment shall deduct and withhold from
				such payment a tax equal to 30 percent of the amount of such payment.</span></p></p><a id="H4B672A2468814ABBB57F66D7E74C5613"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(b) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Requirements for
				waiver of withholding</span>.The requirements of this subsection are met
				with respect to the beneficial owner of a payment if<a id="H24CB609BB1934D878B46E05B424AECD4"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) such beneficial
				owner or the payee provides the withholding agent with either<a id="H8DDF0F7964254AE3B78E7D71E48125CE"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) a certification
				that such beneficial owner does not have any substantial United States owners,
				or</p></p><a id="H925DCAEC35E84134A8C7BA840AA4CAAD"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) the name, address,
				and TIN of each substantial United States owner of such beneficial
				owner,</p></p></p></p><a id="HADB290928A0746D4829139E32D83D551"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) the withholding
				agent does not know, or have reason to know, that any information provided
				under paragraph (1) is incorrect, and</p></p><a id="H85EE1E3E90B44498BF87DED3BA25240A"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(3) the withholding
				agent reports the information provided under paragraph (1)(B) to the Secretary
				in such manner as the Secretary may provide.</p></p></p></p><a id="H9E2E2697F94E414FB66BD867239B2107"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(c) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Exceptions</span>.Subsection
				(a) shall not apply to<a id="H3EFCD4BD92CD46DEAAEDA58EF4B2367C"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) except as
				otherwise provided by the Secretary, any payment beneficially owned by<a id="HC9F7BE31B4A1477EB253C73507204A8D"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) any corporation
				the stock of which is regularly traded on an established securities
				market,</p></p><a id="HD7B55EBD27F742B1A776B401BC858187"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) any corporation
				which is a member of the same expanded affiliated group (as defined in section
				1471(e)(2) without regard to the last sentence thereof) as a corporation
				described in subparagraph (A),</p></p><a id="H3FCC962274CB4C159B08D4AD16C4782A"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(C) any foreign government, any political
				subdivision of a foreign government, or any wholly owned agency or
				instrumentality of any one or more of the foregoing,</p></p><a id="HF75FB46473184D0CB93D7AB0522982D9"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(D) any international
				organization or any wholly owned agency or instrumentality thereof,</p></p><a id="H471460217CF14E69B6720EA618D88DC7"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(E) any foreign
				central bank of issue, or</p></p><a id="H23ED82939CE64987B7D2234AEE232CB1"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(F) any other class of
				persons identified by the Secretary for purposes of this subsection, and</p></p></p></p><a id="H089EA5876DC6456A9CBC287A0C0340D8"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) any class of payments identified by the
				Secretary for purposes of this subsection as posing a low risk of tax
				evasion.</p></p></p></p><a id="H7A5706402B734546B84856301C77382B"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(d) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Non-Financial
				foreign entity</span>.For purposes of this section, the term
				non-financial foreign entity means any foreign entity which is
				not a financial institution (as defined in section 1471(d)(5)).</p></p><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHang"><a href="#H46552F08BBF2450899792A9B2FB4C79D" id="toc-H46552F08BBF2450899792A9B2FB4C79D"><div class="lbexHangWithMargin">
<span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"><a id="H46552F08BBF2450899792A9B2FB4C79D"></a>SEC. 1473. </span><span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"> <span class="lbexAllcap">Definitions</span>.</span>
</div></a></p><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent"><p style="text-align:left">For purposes of this subchapter</p></p><a id="HF6486C07C481471F88CE498415D10726"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">W</span><span class="lbexSmallText">ITHHOLDABLE
				PAYMENT</span>.The term withholdable payment
				means<a id="H66135CD2C3A748B0AF147F4863421D9E"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) any payment of
				interest (including any original issue discount), dividends, rents, salaries,
				wages, premiums, annuities, compensations, remunerations, emoluments, and other
				fixed or determinable annual or periodical gains, profits, and income, if such
				payment is from sources within the United States, and</p></p><a id="H9CACF1C4335249C48804F0244ED165FB"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) any gross proceeds
				from the sale of any property of a type which can produce interest or dividends
				from sources within the United States.</p></p></p></p><a id="H9D08B61C9F294C00AF39C34005611291"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">S</span><span class="lbexSmallText">UBSTANTIAL
				UNITED STATES OWNER</span>.<a id="H54AFAE3052D3474AA1DB7E611A2AB536"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">I</span><span class="lbexSmallText">N
				GENERAL</span>.The term substantial United States owner
				means<a id="H5606DAA238324CBB866537D0051A66E9"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(i) with respect to
				any corporation, any specified United States person which owns, directly or
				indirectly, more than 10 percent of the stock of such corporation (by vote or
				value),</p></p><a id="H946577C070394BB2BFB275CE3D48288B"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(ii) with respect to
				any partnership, any specified United States person which owns, directly or
				indirectly, more than 10 percent of the profits interests or capital interests
				in such partnership, and</p></p><a id="H66E929F19A7B48049CA2ECB961A072CD"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(iii) in the case of a
				trust, any specified United States person treated as an owner of any portion of
				such trust under subpart E of part I of subchapter J of chapter 1.</p></p></p></p><a id="HE8E0C8F0B1D245E6808DD4E2358EEDAC"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">S</span><span class="lbexSmallText">PECIAL RULE FOR
				INVESTMENT VEHICLES</span>.In the
				case of any financial institution described in section 1471(d)(5)(C), clauses
				(i) and (ii) of subparagraph (A) shall be applied by substituting 0
				percent for 10 percent.</p></p></p></p><a id="HB1320AC126F248D6BA5300C21C5A6E0D"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(3) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">S</span><span class="lbexSmallText">PECIFIED UNITED
				STATES PERSON</span>.Except as otherwise provided by the Secretary, the
				term specified United States person means any United States
				person other than<a id="H9CAD6F9B62DF41968C77D73EF700808F"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) any corporation
				the stock of which is regularly traded on an established securities
				market,</p></p><a id="H0B97DEEDE831408ABE402A3CC5DF80CD"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) any corporation
				which is a member of the same expanded affiliated group (as defined in section
				1471(e)(2) without regard to the last sentence thereof) as a corporation
				described in subparagraph (A),</p></p><a id="H38810457B68F4DB4BDE92EF1A9CC0BFB"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(C) any organization exempt from taxation under
				section 501(a) or an individual retirement plan,</p></p><a id="HD5BB2D567BA7485198466BA83D3EC16A"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(D) the United States
				or any wholly owned agency or instrumentality thereof,</p></p><a id="H34681908E8F24527992F883B8A269941"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(E) any State, the
				District of Columbia, any possession of the United States, any political
				subdivision of any of the foregoing, or any wholly owned agency or
				instrumentality of any one or more of the foregoing,</p></p><a id="H378CCB911BFD4156AB3877417C8FEFF2"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(F) any bank (as
				defined in section 581),</p></p><a id="H39285F3FA15D473881948BF8A42A36F5"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(G) any real estate
				investment trust (as defined in section 856),</p></p><a id="H276419B2E4B04298A35265E099F1C4BC"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(H) any regulated
				investment company (as defined in section 851),</p></p><a id="H20BCC15F94F141CD888833B17D516A07"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(I) any common trust
				fund (as defined in section 584(a)), and</p></p><a id="HA712913187EA465E8E30FC0DB8DAA4DB"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(J) any trust
				which<a id="HAE2583CC4C6D444293EA6BA0B25EC91B"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(i) is
				exempt from tax under section 664(c), or</p></p><a id="H400BE1CCE0ED4DBCA52A882226A81CFA"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(ii) is described in
				section 4947(a)(1).</p></p></p></p></p></p><a id="H80D0A6077FF94161AF50BDD29080984A"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(4) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">W</span><span class="lbexSmallText">ITHHOLDING
				AGENT</span>.The term withholding agent means all
				persons, in whatever capacity acting, having the control, receipt, custody,
				disposal, or payment of any withholdable payment.</p></p><a id="H01158F322AAA42F687894571E0A6E00C"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(5) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">F</span><span class="lbexSmallText">OREIGN
				ENTITY</span>.The term foreign entity means any entity
				which is not a United States person.</p></p><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHang"><a href="#H60F8DF697564429EA8D8E0D8CB411CD6" id="toc-H60F8DF697564429EA8D8E0D8CB411CD6"><div class="lbexHangWithMargin">
<span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"><a id="H60F8DF697564429EA8D8E0D8CB411CD6"></a>SEC. 1474. </span><span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"> <span class="lbexAllcap">Special
				rules</span>.</span>
</div></a></p><a id="H3D788A85055E48B3925CC06B5862BAE6"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(a) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Liability for
				withheld tax</span>.Every person
				required to deduct and withhold any tax under this chapter is hereby made
				liable for such tax and is hereby indemnified against the claims and demands of
				any person for the amount of any payments made in accordance with the
				provisions of this chapter.</p></p><a id="HE45C79381B1B4797B91CCA997539E2A2"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(b) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Credits and
				refunds</span>.<a id="HC05E8E254FDB46258482BB9166C47E83"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">I</span><span class="lbexSmallText">N
				GENERAL</span>.Except as provided in paragraph (2), the determination of
				whether any tax deducted and withheld under this chapter results in an
				overpayment shall be made as if such tax had been deducted and withheld under
				subchapter A of chapter 3.</p></p><a id="H84D38D08C47B40ACA799DB8056401C9A"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">S</span><span class="lbexSmallText">PECIAL RULE
				WHERE FOREIGN FINANCIAL INSTITUTION IS BENEFICIAL OWNER OF PAYMENT</span>.<a id="HAB6B81F7F3FC4A13BB0EE19BB1184805"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">I</span><span class="lbexSmallText">N
				GENERAL</span>.In the case of any tax deducted and withheld under
				section 1471(a) from a specified financial institution payment<a id="H45EE177768004D3DA781B191DFDF9F32"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(i) if
				the foreign financial institution referred to in subparagraph (B) with respect
				to such payment is entitled to a reduced rate of tax with respect to such
				payment by reason of any treaty obligation of the United States<a id="HA75DECEE8A264199B847F95F31DD2E5B"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubclause">(I) the amount of any
				credit or refund with respect to such tax shall not exceed the amount of credit
				or refund attributable to such reduction in rate, and</p></p><a id="H70B7B40F9F004CBB8F4499DE2964E099"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubclause">(II) no interest shall
				be allowed or paid with respect to such credit or refund, and</p></p></p></p><a id="H92E663497B62461EAC797399562D3BAE"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(ii) if such foreign
				financial institution is not so entitled, no credit or refund shall be allowed
				or paid with respect to such tax.</p></p></p></p><a id="H06E4FCAB0428443A92C89FFAB4DFA6CB"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">S</span><span class="lbexSmallText">PECIFIED
				FINANCIAL INSTITUTION PAYMENT</span>.The term specified financial
				institution payment means any withholdable payment if the foreign
				financial institution payee referred to in section 1471(a) with respect to such
				payment is the beneficial owner of such payment.</p></p></p></p></p></p><a id="H6F3FC26BAF1E418AB3A7234818A004F1"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(c) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Confidentiality
				of information</span>.<a id="H54FD0529594E4F7E8C7EFF396A1AC677"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">I</span><span class="lbexSmallText">N
				GENERAL</span>.For purposes of this chapter, rules similar to the rules
				of section 3406(f) shall apply.</p></p><a id="H2B983B6E88C745EC946D8D288DE85399"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">D</span><span class="lbexSmallText">ISCLOSURE OF
				LIST OF QUALIFIED FOREIGN FINANCIAL INSTITUTIONS PERMITTED</span>.The
				identity of a foreign financial institution which meets the requirements of
				section 1471(b) shall not be treated as return information for purposes of
				section 6103.</p></p></p></p><a id="H618CD35C24B946C7A9C07B0F7CA742DB"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(d) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Regulations</span>.The
				Secretary shall prescribe such regulations or other guidance as may be
				necessary or appropriate to carry out the purposes of this
				chapter..</p></p></p></p>
<a id="H64915664D07F434DB317E59F81A56280"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(b) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Coordination
			 with other withholding provisions</span>.<a id="H6345F0B403A942A18366FE88FDBFDA82"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">W</span><span class="lbexSmallText">ITHHOLDING OF
			 TAX ON NONRESIDENT ALIENS AND FOREIGN CORPORATIONS</span>.Subsection (c)
			 of section 1441 is amended by adding at the end the following new
			 paragraph:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><a id="HEAF9413D09A44ADB81C86F2CFE64D9EA"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(13) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">W</span><span class="lbexSmallText">ITHHOLDABLE
				PAYMENTS TAXED UNDER CHAPTER 4</span>.No tax shall be required to be deducted and
				withheld under subsection (a) from any amount with respect to which tax is
				required to be deducted and withheld under chapter
				4..</p></p></p></p></p><a id="H6DC1F7C45C9A488C809E6DAE5A52360F"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">W</span><span class="lbexSmallText">ITHHOLDING OF
			 TAX ON DISPOSITIONS OF UNITED STATES REAL PROPERTY
			 INTERESTS</span>.Subsection (b) of section 1445 is amended by adding at
			 the end the following new paragraph:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><a id="H586268D29A7B475CAF316002BE4DC55A"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(10) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">W</span><span class="lbexSmallText">ITHHOLDABLE
				PAYMENTS TAXED UNDER CHAPTER 4</span>.No tax shall be required to be deducted and
				withheld under subsection (a) from any amount with respect to which tax is
				required to be deducted and withheld under chapter
				4..</p></p></p></p></p></p>
<a id="HF58AACE311294BE08637CD42151523B1"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(c) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Clerical
			 amendment</span>.The table of
			 chapters of such Code is amended by adding at the end the following new
			 item:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent"><p></p><span><div style="text-align:center" class="lbexTocDivisionOLC">
<p></p>
<a href="#toc-H7800A27C871C47D79A1BD24909A92FBF" id="H7800A27C871C47D79A1BD24909A92FBF">CHAPTER 4. TAXES TO ENFORCE REPORTING ON CERTAIN FOREIGN
				ACCOUNTS.</a>
</div></span></p></p>
<a id="HED73E965E41F4E60A6C6F44212436C1D"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(d) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Effective
			 date</span>.<a id="H0267D1E1FAE54C76A159B666B067DE42"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">I</span><span class="lbexSmallText">N
			 GENERAL</span>.Except as provided in paragraph (2), the amendments made
			 by this section shall apply to payments made after December 31, 2010.</p></p><a id="H27900C1BCE8A4214A8FF56879BED71BF"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">G</span><span class="lbexSmallText">RANDFATHERED
			 TREATMENT OF CERTAIN OUTSTANDING OBLIGATIONS</span>.The amendments made
			 by this section shall not apply to any obligation outstanding on the date of
			 first committee action, if such obligation<a id="HDB3BA47E357C410F8D20E6696CACE9CC"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) is in bearer form,
			 or</p></p><a id="H5A3D069B2BC74FF68831DC56D787D22D"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) includes (on the
			 date of the issuance of such obligation) a provision under which the issuer
			 would (but for this paragraph) be obligated to make additional payments under
			 such obligation by reason of the amendments made by this section.</p></p></p></p></p>
<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHang"><a href="#HE5673CA625674203A24B258454BDA261" id="toc-HE5673CA625674203A24B258454BDA261"><div class="lbexHangWithMargin">
<span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"><a id="HE5673CA625674203A24B258454BDA261"></a>SEC. 102. </span><span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"> <span class="lbexAllcap">Repeal of
			 certain foreign exceptions to registered bond requirements</span>.</span>
</div></a></p>
<a id="HED321D59F7B6465B879BB13A0569BCC2"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(a) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Repeal of
			 exception to denial of deduction for interest on non-Registered bonds</span>.<a id="H8910EB32A270428FB935D2C4FD77E863"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">I</span><span class="lbexSmallText">N
			 GENERAL</span>.Paragraph (2) of
			 section 163(f) is amended by striking subparagraph (B) and by redesignating
			 subparagraph (C) as subparagraph (B).</p></p><a id="H4F66EEA5CAB04481B4F27C6F479A236A"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">C</span><span class="lbexSmallText">ONFORMING
			 AMENDMENTS</span>.<a id="HE56CF8D925E84DAF876BF4D9DDE7F2AE"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) Subparagraph (A)
			 of section 163(f)(2) is amended by inserting or at the end of
			 clause (ii), by striking , or at the end of clause (iii) and
			 inserting a period, and by striking clause (iv).</p></p><a id="HA13838C838F14A6ABDF5C693798AA900"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) Subparagraph (B)
			 of section 163(f)(2), as redesignated by paragraph (1), is amended<a id="H470BA11F52B0477D98FE5054AFC962A5"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(i) by
			 striking , and subparagraph (B), in the matter preceding clause
			 (i), and</p></p><a id="HEEE74E357E3A48DAA2CB23F0200903C8"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(ii) by
			 amending clause (i) to read as follows:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentClause"><a id="HFA3CCF42BFE642E7B6FF258F7E667F82"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(i) such obligation is of a type which the
				Secretary has determined by regulations to be used frequently in avoiding
				Federal taxes,
				and.</p></p></p></p></p></p></p><a id="H700C40DE4EBF4C058A50E357D996D719"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(C) Sections
			 165(j)(2)(A) and 1287(b)(1) are each amended by striking except that
			 clause (iv) of subparagraph (A), and subparagraph (B), of such section shall
