<a id="H121C293087AC4AF7B729DB2A60FBC970"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(b) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Repeal of
			 treatment as portfolio debt</span>.<a id="H8233407287BF407ABB3B30DB3FF7269B"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">I</span><span class="lbexSmallText">N
			 GENERAL</span>.Paragraph (2) of section 871(h) is amended to read as
			 follows:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><a id="H6862141545BB498ABB51E0070540F44C"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">P</span><span class="lbexSmallText">ORTFOLIO
				INTEREST</span>.For purposes of this
				subsection, the term portfolio interest means any interest
				(including original issue discount) which<a id="HF3BDBEB0AD6C42F7AD37D751C9748863"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) would be subject
				to tax under subsection (a) but for this subsection, and</p></p><a id="H0CE6AACA11004F089C499CD3FCC86484"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) is paid on an
				obligation<a id="H5133A0AFE29F4D12AE5E17C03D1C4966"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(i) which is in
				registered form, and</p></p><a id="HC5F8CAD132C04F6AB5AFD787AE2AAF13"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(ii) with respect to which the United States
				person who would otherwise be required to deduct and withhold tax from such
				interest under section 1441(a) receives a statement (which meets the
				requirements of paragraph (5)) that the beneficial owner of the obligation is
				not a United States
				person..</p></p></p></p></p></p></p></p></p><a id="H84071D05E94E4B9A8B05EA4848869801"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">C</span><span class="lbexSmallText">ONFORMING
			 AMENDMENT</span>.Section
			 871(h)(3)(A) is amended by striking subparagraph (A) or (B)
			 of.</p></p></p>
<a id="H254E2A479CDF483DA5B53B6CA8CEEF6E"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(c) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Repeal of
			 exception to requirement that Treasury obligations be in registered
			 form</span>.<a id="H93F24C71820B44578DE4A1142DF7CD8B"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">I</span><span class="lbexSmallText">N
			 GENERAL</span>.Subsection (g) of section 3121 of title 31, United States
			 Code, is amended by striking paragraph (2) and by redesignating paragraphs (3)
			 and (4) as paragraphs (2) and (3), respectively.</p></p><a id="HA61EB79917FD40DC9F1CF1EE6D53DE11"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">C</span><span class="lbexSmallText">ONFORMING
			 AMENDMENTS</span>.Paragraph (1) of section 3121(g) of such title is
			 amended<a id="H7A8CD143E361472A94AFEC975A626927"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) by adding
			 or at the end of subparagraph (A),</p></p><a id="HA48795ACA1C04B6DA3DEC2A29ADE0147"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) by striking
			 ; or at the end of subparagraph (B) and inserting a period,
			 and</p></p><a id="H1F24317543CE4100917D219898C673B8"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(C) by striking
			 subparagraph (C).</p></p></p></p></p>
<a id="H402BCFB4DF3145FBA2B6610228DCF540"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(d) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Effective
			 date</span>.The amendments made by this section shall apply to
			 obligations issued after the date which is 180 days after the date of the
			 enactment of this Act.</p>
<a id="H8E0966FB328A42988C8349F497B74778"></a><p><div style="text-align:center"><a href="#H8E0966FB328A42988C8349F497B74778" id="toc-H8E0966FB328A42988C8349F497B74778"><span class="lbexTitleLevelOLC">TITLE II</span><span class="lbexTitleLevelOLC"><span style="text-align:center"></span><span class="lbexAllcap">Under reporting
			 with respect to foreign assets</span></span></a></div></p>
<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHang"><a href="#HBD3B64DF74D84602B03F4B94C3CE9BAA" id="toc-HBD3B64DF74D84602B03F4B94C3CE9BAA"><div class="lbexHangWithMargin">
<span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"><a id="HBD3B64DF74D84602B03F4B94C3CE9BAA"></a>SEC. 201. </span><span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"> <span class="lbexAllcap">Disclosure of
			 information with respect to foreign financial assets</span>.</span>
</div></a></p>
<a id="H9473F8455DEE47FCB8C1124A9FDC69DE"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(a) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">In
			 general</span>.Subpart A of part III of subchapter A of chapter 61 is
			 amended by inserting after section 6038C the following new section:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHang"><a href="#HC492DE71AB3D4A57B88985D2DA9FE85E" id="toc-HC492DE71AB3D4A57B88985D2DA9FE85E"><div class="lbexHangWithMargin">
<span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"><a id="HC492DE71AB3D4A57B88985D2DA9FE85E"></a>SEC. 6038D. </span><span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"> <span class="lbexAllcap">Information
				with respect to foreign financial assets</span>.</span>
</div></a></p><a id="HFF3FBE34C1694C76823FC14268B916C0"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(a) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">In
				general</span>.Any individual who, during any taxable year, holds any
				interest in a specified foreign financial asset shall attach to such persons
				return of tax imposed by subtitle A for such taxable year the information
				described in subsection (c) with respect to each such asset if the aggregate
				value of all such assets exceeds $50,000 (or such higher dollar amount as the
				Secretary may prescribe).</p></p><a id="HDEBA7C59AE154B16BC2F3778D996D352"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(b) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Specified
				foreign financial assets</span>.For purposes of this section, the term
				specified foreign financial asset means<a id="H2F80C780F8FC49BFBB5F6414F42F5B83"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) any financial account (as defined in
				section 1471(d)(2)) maintained by a foreign financial institution (as defined
				in section 1471(d)(4)), and</p></p><a id="H39820418E1AC45E2B1919EA3E1C94F12"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) any of the
				following assets which are not held in an account maintained by a financial
				institution (as defined in section 1471(d)(5))<a id="H6D248620E1534DDCAB2FDB2DC4C4C8EE"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) any stock or
				security issued by a person other than a United States person,</p></p><a id="HE59B68555CA04C2AA0E209B1934730CA"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) any financial instrument or contract held
				for investment that has an issuer or counterparty which is other than a United
				States person, and</p></p><a id="HD13B91401973427CB39BA4DBAC3E0AF3"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(C) any interest in a foreign entity (as
				defined in section 1473).</p></p></p></p></p></p><a id="HBCA89FFC0D594C6BA5989657994BD37D"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(c) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Required
				information</span>.The information described in this subsection with
				respect to any asset is:<a id="HBBD639B08A664DE7AE3DC3BFA91EB26A"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) In the case of any
				account, the name and address of the financial institution in which such
				account is maintained and the number of such account.</p></p><a id="HBE7282BF303243508AF7C888EEA77D0C"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) In the case of any
				stock or security, the name and address of the issuer and such information as
				is necessary to identify the class or issue of which such stock or security is
				a part.</p></p><a id="H495D0CD7391A4CDE877F9719499B1AA7"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(3) In the case of any
				other instrument, contract, or interest<a id="HA43B8410E5C74C52BC5E377602523CC9"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) such information
				as is necessary to identify such instrument, contract, or interest, and</p></p><a id="HB4D8E1201206485BA8FC4910E3E4BE0D"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) the names and
				addresses of all issuers and counterparties with respect to such instrument,
				contract, or interest.</p></p></p></p><a id="H89E0541AAD9B4AE482F901115843B875"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(4) The maximum value
				of the asset during the taxable year.</p></p></p></p><a id="H9E4D7BF3E27A44BD9EF9A5BD29F5F0D2"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(d) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Penalty for
				failure To disclose</span>.<a id="HE57C8FA38245410BBC6616C2C3C8E5F1"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">I</span><span class="lbexSmallText">N
				GENERAL</span>.If any individual fails to furnish the information
				described in subsection (c) with respect to any taxable year at the time and in
				the manner described in subsection (a), such person shall pay a penalty of
				$10,000.</p></p><a id="HDBE2F8F4D0CF4B9981B1A0E2E4EABFAE"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">I</span><span class="lbexSmallText">NCREASE IN
				PENALTY WHERE FAILURE CONTINUES AFTER NOTIFICATION</span>.If any failure
				described in paragraph (1) continues for more than 90 days after the day on
				which the Secretary mails notice of such failure to the individual, such
				individual shall pay a penalty (in addition to the penalties under paragraph
				(1)) of $10,000 for each 30-day period (or fraction thereof) during which such
				failure continues after the expiration of such 90-day period. The penalty
				imposed under this paragraph with respect to any failure shall not exceed
				$50,000.</p></p></p></p><a id="H2701E48C9D2545029485F51DC76B4896"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(e) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Presumption that
				value of specified foreign financial assets exceeds dollar
				threshold</span>.If<a id="H19DEBBB629A64798BF41FD714710ADAC"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) the Secretary
				determines that an individual has an interest in one or more specified foreign
				financial assets, and</p></p><a id="H3EBAABC6EB124A3C8A2145239E20EDF6"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) such individual
				does not provide sufficient information to demonstrate the aggregate value of
				such assets,</p></p><p></p><span class="lbexNonIndentSubsection">then the
				aggregate value of such assets shall be treated as being in excess of $50,000
				(or such higher dollar amount as the Secretary prescribes for purposes of
				subsection (a)) for purposes of assessing the penalties imposed under this
				section.</span></p></p><a id="H75D15771198B4180B6F545BAC28767D7"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(f) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Application to
				certain entities</span>.To the extent provided by the Secretary in
				regulations or other guidance, the provisions of this section shall apply to
				any domestic entity which is formed or availed of for purposes of holding,
				directly or indirectly, specified foreign financial assets, in the same manner
				as if such entity were an individual.</p></p><a id="H086ADF60025340BD8AC6E5C47BC6C8FA"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(g) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Reasonable cause
				exception</span>.No penalty shall be imposed by this section on any
				failure which is shown to be due to reasonable cause and not due to willful
				neglect. The fact that a foreign jurisdiction would impose a civil or criminal
				penalty on the taxpayer (or any other person) for disclosing the required
				information is not reasonable cause.</p></p><a id="H422A009070264FA8A2D361F518848240"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(h) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Regulations</span>.The Secretary shall prescribe such
				regulations or other guidance as may be necessary or appropriate to carry out
				the purposes of this section, including regulations or other guidance which
				provide appropriate exceptions from the application of this section in the case
				of<a id="H4E6C6914DD564797962F8686E5116762"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) classes of assets
				identified by the Secretary, including any assets with respect to which the
				Secretary determines that disclosure under this section would be duplicative of
				other disclosures, and</p></p><a id="H1E6ECBAA363A4AF3983D3D2E11A52015"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) nonresident
				aliens..</p></p></p></p></p></p>
<a id="H5B5571BA22EC4D81B6974F54FE9403F1"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(b) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Clerical
			 amendment</span>.The table of
			 sections for subpart A of part III of subchapter A of chapter 61 is amended by
			 inserting after the item relating to section 6038C the following new
			 item:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent"><p></p><span><span class="lbexTocSectionOLC"><br><a href="#toc-HC492DE71AB3D4A57B88985D2DA9FE85E" id="HC492DE71AB3D4A57B88985D2DA9FE85E">Sec.6038D.Information with respect to foreign financial
				assets..</a></span></span></p></p>
<a id="H41E07197335B43C292BB695A61B925D4"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(c) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Effective
			 date</span>.The amendments made by
			 this section shall apply to taxable years beginning after the date of the
			 enactment of this Act.</p>
<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHang"><a href="#H0B0EDC14BFE54979A3EFC5B5CF193E50" id="toc-H0B0EDC14BFE54979A3EFC5B5CF193E50"><div class="lbexHangWithMargin">
<span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"><a id="H0B0EDC14BFE54979A3EFC5B5CF193E50"></a>SEC. 202.</span><span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"> <span class="lbexAllcap">Penalties for
			 underpayments attributable to undisclosed foreign financial assets</span>.</span>
</div></a></p>
<a id="HA96A27C324374777B4151BFD5644732E"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(a) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">In
			 general</span>.Section 6662 is amended<a id="H7E3DF48D3064464F86A19C041033B499"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) in subsection (b), by inserting after
			 paragraph (5) the following new paragraph:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><a id="H157F00D6E6A641DF8FFD0DDC7FD56069"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(6) Any undisclosed foreign financial asset
				understatement.,
				and</p></p></p></p></p><a id="HD36895064BF643E0B35DBBF37CDE5649"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p class="lbexIndentParagraph" style="text-align:left"><span class="lbexIndent">(2) by adding at the
			 end the following new subsection:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><a id="H40775BCDE0AB46788266996B3BA7775B"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(i) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Undisclosed
				foreign financial asset understatement</span>.<a id="H3E1B3B9071E94872B9927F44A6C8B23D"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">I</span><span class="lbexSmallText">N
				GENERAL</span>.For purposes of this
				section, the term undisclosed foreign financial asset
				understatement means, for any taxable year, the portion of the
				understatement for such taxable year which is attributable to any transaction
				involving an undisclosed foreign financial asset.</p></p><a id="H73399AB931D64F3386913A859C5A44BD"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">U</span><span class="lbexSmallText">NDISCLOSED
				FOREIGN FINANCIAL ASSET</span>.For purposes of this subsection, the term
				undisclosed foreign financial asset means, with respect to any
				taxable year, any asset with respect to which information was required to be
				provided under section 6038, 6038B, 6038D, 6046A, or 6048 for such taxable year
				but was not provided by the taxpayer as required under the provisions of those
				sections.</p></p><a id="H979E0059F2B14E5FA381A77698A8885D"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(3) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">I</span><span class="lbexSmallText">NCREASE IN
				PENALTY FOR UNDISCLOSED FOREIGN FINANCIAL ASSET
				UNDERSTATEMENTS</span>.In the case of any portion of an underpayment
				which is attributable to any undisclosed foreign financial asset
				understatement, subsection (a) shall be applied with respect to such portion by
				substituting 40 percent for 20
				percent..</p></p></p></p></p></span></p><p class="lbexIndentParagraph" style="text-align:left"></p></p></p>
<a id="HCF8C05CAE7264FF19EF3F7C80CBF9EA0"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(b) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Effective
			 Date</span>.The amendments made by
			 this section shall apply to taxable years beginning after the date of the
			 enactment of this Act.</p>
<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHang"><a href="#H07FB069A9B57400390231943EA7D5887" id="toc-H07FB069A9B57400390231943EA7D5887"><div class="lbexHangWithMargin">
<span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"><a id="H07FB069A9B57400390231943EA7D5887"></a>SEC. 203. </span><span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"> <span class="lbexAllcap">Modification of
			 statute of limitations for significant omission of income in connection with
			 foreign assets</span>.</span>
</div></a></p>
<a id="H963189366BDC499B81D86769D8CBAF9F"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(a) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Extension of
			 statute of limitations</span>.<a id="H7BEBF957BA2B4AD4BFF138A1866E8127"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">I</span><span class="lbexSmallText">N
			 GENERAL</span>.Paragraph (1) of
			 section 6501(e) is amended by redesignating subparagraphs (A) and (B) as
			 subparagraphs (B) and (C), respectively, and by inserting before subparagraph
			 (B) (as so redesignated) the following new subparagraph:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><a id="HA0178E4CE2464068A9A6316EAC66A630"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">G</span><span class="lbexSmallText">ENERAL
				RULE</span>.If the taxpayer omits
				from gross income an amount properly includible therein and<a id="H10909FDBEB15490AB178461ABF394F83"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(i) such amount is in
				excess of 25 percent of the amount of gross income stated in the return,
				or</p></p><a id="H393DEE7B1A8542C7BF25C81A2BE8100D"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(ii) such
				amount<a id="HABD9C79451D744858E1BB1A70AD6D959"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubclause">(I) is attributable to
				one or more assets with respect to which information is required to be reported
				under section 6038D (or would be so required if such section were applied
				without regard to the dollar threshold specified in subsection (a) thereof and
				without regard to any exceptions provided pursuant to subsection (h)(1)
				thereof), and</p></p><a id="HA087A4D948D24FCA89D3F0BAFDCD3F7F"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubclause">(II) is in excess of
				$5,000,</p></p></p></p><p class="nolbexIndentSubpar">the tax
				may be assessed, or a proceeding in court for collection of such tax may be
				begun without assessment, at any time within 6 years after the return was
				filed..</p></p></p></p></p></p><a id="H58D02C5ED59B4A9B803B02FCDAC4FE91"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">C</span><span class="lbexSmallText">ONFORMING
			 AMENDMENTS</span>.<a id="H6B20B03FB7F24128BA48C3BE87481F0A"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) Subparagraph (B)
			 of section 6501(e)(1), as redesignated by paragraph (1), is amended by striking
			 all that precedes clause (i) and inserting the following:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentClause"><a id="H03BF68FF327A4E179A6BDBF7E2275C53"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">D</span><span class="lbexSmallText">ETERMINATION OF
				GROSS INCOME</span>.For purposes of
				subparagraph
				(A).</p></p></p></p></p><a id="H3A457F0382A04917AAB4FE4E1A3EEACB"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) Paragraph (2) of
			 section 6229(c) is amended by striking which is in excess of 25 percent
			 of the amount of gross income stated in its return and inserting
			 and such amount is described in clause (i) or (ii) of section
			 6501(e)(1)(A).</p></p></p></p></p>
<a id="H2C0C5170006246A18DE5E4F568A4BEBB"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(b) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Additional
			 reports subject to extended period</span>.Paragraph (8) of section
			 6501(c) is amended<a id="H4591634A562A4E5AB1A2EC589A3A51E6"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) by inserting
			 pursuant to an election under section 1295(b) or before
			 under section 6038,</p></p><a id="HF88C30FF2D0A4356BB4CE3B9E52B23C2"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) by inserting
			 1298(f), before 6038, and</p></p><a id="HA0E22D4953044DBFA206C31DD619022E"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(3) by inserting
			 6038D, after 6038B,.</p></p></p>
<a id="HFA986016FD54499190F242BF8B196A43"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(c) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Clarifications
			 related to failure To disclose foreign transfers</span>.Paragraph (8) of section 6501(c) is amended
			 by striking event and inserting tax return,
			 event,.</p>
<a id="HF20DD604B41D487B8071B37B0732D0EF"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(d) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Effective
			 date</span>.The amendments made by
			 this section shall apply to<a id="H93BBF0BB1DFD4C59A6E7B190A66DCC34"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) returns filed
			 after the date of the enactment of this Act; and</p></p><a id="HC19729574E0D4AFCB9BDC5829D764CBF"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) returns filed on
			 or before such date if the period specified in section 6501 of the Internal
			 Revenue Code of 1986 (determined without regard to such amendments) for
			 assessment of such taxes has not expired as of such date.</p></p></p>
<a id="H5262DD62C5334F18AFEE8FFDF8AC2FC0"></a><p><div style="text-align:center"><a href="#H5262DD62C5334F18AFEE8FFDF8AC2FC0" id="toc-H5262DD62C5334F18AFEE8FFDF8AC2FC0"><span class="lbexTitleLevelOLC">TITLE III</span><span class="lbexTitleLevelOLC"><span style="text-align:center"></span><span class="lbexAllcap">Other disclosure
			 provisions </span></span></a></div></p>
<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHang"><a href="#HB0DA248DE26C4EA193C806B397645253" id="toc-HB0DA248DE26C4EA193C806B397645253"><div class="lbexHangWithMargin">
<span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"><a id="HB0DA248DE26C4EA193C806B397645253"></a>SEC. 301. </span><span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"> <span class="lbexAllcap">Disclosure of
			 assistance in acquiring or forming a foreign entity</span>.</span>
</div></a></p>
<a id="H5F6CB0B97C6D4D4DA15259469BA512A7"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(a) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">In
			 general</span>.Subchapter B of
			 chapter 61 is amended by redesignating section 6116 as section 6117 and by
			 inserting after 6115 the following new section:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHang"><a href="#H3252174CB81A4451B3F8A6059C1C9BD6" id="toc-H3252174CB81A4451B3F8A6059C1C9BD6"><div class="lbexHangWithMargin">
<span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"><a id="H3252174CB81A4451B3F8A6059C1C9BD6"></a>SEC. 6116. </span><span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"> <span class="lbexAllcap">Disclosure of
				assistance in acquiring or forming a foreign entity</span>.</span>
</div></a></p><a id="H0A8AE6FC80C34A5DAAA1086854921455"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(a) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">In
				general</span>.Each material advisor
				with respect to any foreign entity transaction shall make a return (in such
				form as the Secretary may prescribe) setting forth<a id="H1AEB44F2C08C492DBAC6639B1D430C60"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) the identity of
				the foreign entity referred to in subsection (d),</p></p><a id="HB41E5C32D3D54D33A7709B7F35C090A3"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) the identity of
				the citizen or resident of the United States referred to in subsection (d),
				and</p></p><a id="HC3C32A8456134E5AA70138C2BB554DFD"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(3) such other
				information as the Secretary may prescribe.</p></p><p></p><span class="lbexNonIndentSubsection">Such
				return shall be filed not later than the date specified by the
				Secretary.</span></p></p><a id="H00D52D9C3249460A8237A4E16D9AB6E8"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(b) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Penalty for
				nondisclosure</span>.Any person who is required to file a return under
				subsection (a) with respect to any foreign entity transaction and fails to file
				such return on or before the date prescribed therefor (or files false or
				incomplete information with respect to such transaction) shall pay a penalty
				equal to the greater of<a id="H9EFE3808288A4080B8F89186407529C5"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) $10,000, or</p></p><a id="H00CD53847CF8404AA9D7E3F182DC9676"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) 50 percent of the
				gross income derived by such person with respect to aid, assistance or advice
				which is provided with respect to such transaction before the date the return
				is filed under subsection (a).</p></p></p></p><a id="H6A12247613504244AB8C954197D1553D"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(c) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Material
				advisor</span>.For purposes of this section, the term material
				advisor means any person<a id="H93750EA6B80A4F6A92637C7827F7722F"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) who provides any
				material aid, assistance, or advice with respect to carrying out one or more
				foreign entity transactions, and</p></p><a id="H9FFB0C0267174F7880D72B8D8D8C8BC0"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) who directly or
				indirectly derives gross income in excess of $100,000 for providing such aid,
				assistance or advice during the calendar year.</p></p></p></p><a id="H4DDCD89391034B8F966F079F1EDD6B85"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(d) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Foreign entity
				transaction</span>.For purposes of this section, the term foreign
				entity transaction means the direct or indirect acquisition of any
				interest in a foreign entity (including any interest acquired in connection
				with the formation of such entity) if any citizen or resident of the United
				States is required to file a report under section 6038, 6038B, 6046, 6046A, or
				6048 in connection with such acquisition.</p></p><a id="H6673B37CE9644C1D9202553B83DA9F6A"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(e) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Reasonable cause
				exception</span>.No penalty shall be imposed by this section on any
				failure which is shown to be due to reasonable cause and not due to willful
				neglect.</p></p><a id="H7C2D10CAC9524ADC85D099A6A77263BE"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(f) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Regulations</span>.The
				Secretary may prescribe regulations or other guidance which provide<a id="H12E5268393264356AC8B239568473DEA"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) that only 1 person shall be required to
				meet the requirements of subsection (a) in cases in which 2 or more persons
				would otherwise be required to meet such requirements,</p></p><a id="H33907754059843139CA1EC55BB755F05"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) exemptions from
				the requirements of this section, and</p></p><a id="HC6D7AB9DA4E844F480DB1E4EAD840AF1"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(3) such rules as may
				be necessary or appropriate to carry out the purposes of this
				section..</p></p></p></p></p></p>
<a id="HCCE67493442C4A2AA1EE38D619290153"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(b) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Clerical
			 amendment</span>.The table of
			 sections for subchapter B of chapter 61 is amended by redesignating the item
			 relating to section 6116 as an item relating to section 6117 and by inserting
			 after the item relating to section 6115 the following new item:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent"><p></p><span><span class="lbexTocSectionOLC"><br><a href="#toc-H3252174CB81A4451B3F8A6059C1C9BD6" id="H3252174CB81A4451B3F8A6059C1C9BD6">Sec.6116.Disclosure of assistance in acquiring or forming a
				foreign
				entity..</a></span></span></p></p>
<a id="H4FF340298EEF40D082CFE46DE5974F88"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(c) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Effective
			 date</span>.The amendments made by this section shall apply to aid,
			 assistance, and advice provided after the date of the enactment of this
			 Act.</p>
<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHang"><a href="#H9A7F25C14C1A43E0A3261D2FC5BF4A80" id="toc-H9A7F25C14C1A43E0A3261D2FC5BF4A80"><div class="lbexHangWithMargin">
<span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"><a id="H9A7F25C14C1A43E0A3261D2FC5BF4A80"></a>SEC. 302. </span><span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"> <span class="lbexAllcap">Reporting of
			 activities with respect to passive foreign investment companies</span>.</span>
</div></a></p>
<a id="HF5785D5640B449C1893D381185AD13FE"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(a) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">In
			 general</span>.Section 1298 is amended by redesignating subsection (f)
			 as subsection (g) and by inserting after subsection (e) the following new
			 subsection:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent"><a id="H7C7B8D56072E43E8B6D5719A3B33D045"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(f) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Reporting
				requirement</span>.Each person who is a shareholder of a passive foreign
				investment company shall file an annual report containing such information as
				the Secretary may
				require..</p></p></p></p>
<a id="H165AF195D93241AF952FFD21F68F5120"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(b) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Conforming
			 amendment</span>.Subsection (e) of section 1291 is amended by striking
			 , (d), and (f) and inserting and (d).</p>
<a id="H7390F5DED3614250A9A8672499D9CB15"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(c) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Effective
			 date</span>.The amendments made by this section take effect on the date
			 of the enactment of this Act.</p>
<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHang"><a href="#HD548513EBE1D4CDCB6AE1D1D93CEFF12" id="toc-HD548513EBE1D4CDCB6AE1D1D93CEFF12"><div class="lbexHangWithMargin">
<span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"><a id="HD548513EBE1D4CDCB6AE1D1D93CEFF12"></a>SEC. 303. </span><span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"> <span class="lbexAllcap">Secretary
			 permitted to require financial institutions to file certain returns related to
			 withholding on foreign transfers electronically</span>.</span>
</div></a></p>
<a id="H0372F3BABA45406498E4916552ED1B3D"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(a) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">In
			 general</span>.Subsection (e) of
			 section 6011 is amended by adding at the end the following new
			 paragraph:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent"><a id="H309C8C980D9B4C2CBC044FAFABB9824C"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(3) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">S</span><span class="lbexSmallText">PECIAL RULE FOR
				RETURNS FILED BY FINANCIAL INSTITUTIONS WITH RESPECT TO WITHHOLDING ON FOREIGN
				TRANSFERS</span>.Paragraph (2)(A)
				shall not apply to any return filed by a financial institution (as defined in
				section 1471(d)(5)) with respect to tax for which such institution is made
				liable under section 1461 or
				1474(a)..</p></p></p></p>
<a id="HC3F62DEAB813483982479F1CE48C36E5"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(b) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Effective
			 date</span>.The amendment made by this section shall apply to returns
			 the due date for which (determined without regard to extensions) is after the
			 date of the enactment of this Act.</p>
<a id="HB3AE27AA570546AEBC7E4C8D7338FF20"></a><p><div style="text-align:center"><a href="#HB3AE27AA570546AEBC7E4C8D7338FF20" id="toc-HB3AE27AA570546AEBC7E4C8D7338FF20"><span class="lbexTitleLevelOLC">TITLE IV</span><span class="lbexTitleLevelOLC"><span style="text-align:center"></span><span class="lbexAllcap">Provisions
			 related to foreign trusts</span></span></a></div></p>
<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHang"><a href="#H15710B5859AB435CBAED79ABB9DCAFC3" id="toc-H15710B5859AB435CBAED79ABB9DCAFC3"><div class="lbexHangWithMargin">
<span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"><a id="H15710B5859AB435CBAED79ABB9DCAFC3"></a>SEC. 401. </span><span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"> <span class="lbexAllcap">Clarifications
			 with respect to foreign trusts which are treated as having a United States
			 beneficiary</span>.</span>
</div></a></p>
<a id="HDFDB089FF00D48D0A4F571E0BCA14D3D"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(a) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">In
			 general</span>.Paragraph (1) of
			 section 679(c) is amended by adding at the end the following:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent"><p class="nolbexIndentParagraph">For
				purposes of subparagraph (A), an amount shall be treated as accumulated for the
				benefit of a United States person even if the United States persons interest
				in the trust is contingent on a future
				event..</p></p></p>
<a id="HB256B2B0D1BA4E279CE9DDD587A675FB"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(b) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Clarification
			 regarding discretion To identify beneficiaries</span>.Subsection (c) of
			 section 679 is amended by adding at the end the following new paragraph:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent"><a id="H0CF0B34D507F47FEB85C6158C785596B"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(4) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">S</span><span class="lbexSmallText">PECIAL RULE IN
				CASE OF DISCRETION TO IDENTIFY BENEFICIARIES</span>.For purposes of paragraph (1)(A), if any
				person has the discretion (by authority given in the trust agreement, by power
				of appointment, or otherwise) of making a distribution from the trust to, or
				for the benefit of, any person, such trust shall be treated as having a
				beneficiary who is a United States person unless<a id="H5784517875B2412FA26CADAE2CD35299"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) the terms of the
				trust specifically identify the class of persons to whom such distributions may
				be made, and</p></p><a id="HA3089B0AD9DD4475B91188D13D4868DF"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) none of those
				persons are United States persons during the taxable
				year..</p></p></p></p></p></p>
<a id="H3CB7DE149E074307B6BF205187F3E1C1"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(c) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Clarification
			 that certain agreements and understandings are terms of the
			 trust</span>.Subsection (c) of section 679, as amended by subsection
			 (b), is amended by adding at the end the following new paragraph:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent"><a id="HE9671BDC8BB34C2EBDEBD614834E856C"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(5) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">C</span><span class="lbexSmallText">ERTAIN
				AGREEMENTS AND UNDERSTANDINGS TREATED AS TERMS OF THE TRUST</span>.For
				purposes of paragraph (1)(A), if any United States person who directly or
				indirectly transfers property to the trust is directly or indirectly involved
				in any agreement or understanding (whether written, oral, or otherwise) that
				may result in the income or corpus of the trust being paid or accumulated to or
				for the benefit of a United States person, such agreement or understanding
				shall be treated as a term of the
				trust..</p></p></p></p>
<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHang"><a href="#H1161210BDFB84F4EA0B6200CBE6D5D20" id="toc-H1161210BDFB84F4EA0B6200CBE6D5D20"><div class="lbexHangWithMargin">
<span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"><a id="H1161210BDFB84F4EA0B6200CBE6D5D20"></a>SEC. 402. </span><span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"> <span class="lbexAllcap">Presumption
			 that foreign trust has United States beneficiary</span>.</span>
</div></a></p>
<a id="HE0F20B1303B84E669BB0FBBB29A4370F"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(a) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">In
			 general</span>.Section 679 is
			 amended by redesignating subsection (d) as subsection (e) and inserting after
			 subsection (c) the following new subsection:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent"><a id="HC28198123B2E4FADA5B840AE2FDB6A8D"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(d) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Presumption that
				foreign trust has United States beneficiary</span>.If a United States person directly or
				indirectly transfers property to a foreign trust (other than a trust described
				in section 6048(a)(3)(B)(ii)), such trust shall be presumed to have a United
				States beneficiary for purposes of applying this section to such transfer
				unless such person<a id="H880591B7968B4F658B4B1A3925F4C424"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) submits such
				information to the Secretary as the Secretary may require with respect to such
				transfer, and</p></p><a id="H11000D8030704135AB2BB4D3BC7CB193"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) demonstrates to
				the satisfaction of the Secretary that such trust satisfies the requirements of
				subparagraphs (A) and (B) of subsection
				(c)(1)..</p></p></p></p></p></p>
<a id="H0BEB71D822F840909B6097EA2C704963"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(b) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Effective
			 date</span>.The amendments made by this section shall apply to transfers
			 of property after the date of the enactment of this Act.</p>
<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHang"><a href="#H2490B08235284E958F8696E93813B1E0" id="toc-H2490B08235284E958F8696E93813B1E0"><div class="lbexHangWithMargin">
<span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"><a id="H2490B08235284E958F8696E93813B1E0"></a>SEC. 403. </span><span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"> <span class="lbexAllcap">Uncompensated
			 use of trust property treated as a distribution</span>.</span>
</div></a></p>
<a id="H067BF3D49A1145F38F302F34DA8F15A1"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(a) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">In
			 general</span>.Paragraph (1) of section 643(i) is amended<a id="H25D26A19A2F143518455EAF204F7D5DD"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) by striking
			 directly or indirectly to and inserting (or permits the
			 use of any other trust property) directly or indirectly to or by,
			 and</p></p><a id="HB3596B14BF664A038373F9C363A559F9"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) by inserting
			 (or the fair market value of the use of such property) after
			 the amount of such loan.</p></p></p>
<a id="H808CD4C967A944D59C52442AD61BFA72"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(b) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Exception for
			 compensated use</span>.Paragraph (2) of section 643(i) is amended by
			 adding at the end the following new subparagraph:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent"><a id="H8F59B0F9B52246EEAD3E2040524F7B1A"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(E) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">E</span><span class="lbexSmallText">XCEPTION FOR
				COMPENSATED USE OF PROPERTY</span>.In the case of the use of any trust
				property other than a loan of cash or marketable securities, paragraph (1)
				shall not apply to the extent that the trust is paid the fair market value of
				such use within a reasonable period of time of such
				use..</p></p></p></p>
<a id="H1A2E4F83CED74774A147759B7561E0A5"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(c) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Application to
			 grantor trusts</span>.Subsection (c) of section 679, as amended by
			 section 401, is amended by adding at the end the following new
			 paragraph:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent"><a id="H8FB7E93C302B47AC9B095F3BB44BAD43"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(6) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">U</span><span class="lbexSmallText">NCOMPENSATED
				USE OF TRUST PROPERTY TREATED AS A PAYMENT</span>.For purposes of this subsection, a loan of
				cash or marketable securities (or the use of any other trust property) directly
				or indirectly to or by any United States person (whether or not a beneficiary
				under the terms of the trust) shall be treated as paid or accumulated for the
				benefit of a United States person. The preceding sentence shall not apply to
				the extent that the United States person repays the loan at a market rate of
				interest (or pays the fair market value of the use of such property) within a
				reasonable period of
				time..</p></p></p></p>
<a id="H5F23594ED6404462A6E1B5645C4F909D"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(d) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Conforming
			 amendments</span>.Paragraph (3) of section 643(i) is amended<a id="H214E50DC968C42ECB9E39B3D5881DE23"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) by inserting
			 (or use of property) after If any loan,</p></p><a id="HAC927607C47D4318B8B28879B17BFE50"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) by inserting
			 or the return of such property before shall be
			 disregarded, and</p></p><a id="HCC4F7C3466784453A11D0283B8040FAB"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(3) by striking
			 <span class="lbexAllcapnormal">regarding loan
			 principal</span> in the heading thereof.</p></p></p>
<a id="HE04BCB0D8A2A4EC791F676B595BAC0D1"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(e) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Effective
			 date</span>.The amendments made by
			 this section shall apply to loans made, and uses of property, after the date of
			 the enactment of this Act.</p>
<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHang"><a href="#HFD65816F0A1B4C46AC8E07CDEB2267C8" id="toc-HFD65816F0A1B4C46AC8E07CDEB2267C8"><div class="lbexHangWithMargin">
<span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"><a id="HFD65816F0A1B4C46AC8E07CDEB2267C8"></a>SEC. 404. </span><span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"> <span class="lbexAllcap">Reporting
			 requirement of United States owners of foreign trusts</span>.</span>
</div></a></p>
<a id="H7CCA1424899E420FB37FB74738E90021"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(a) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">In
			 general</span>.Paragraph (1) of
			 section 6048(b) is amended by inserting shall submit such information as
			 the Secretary may prescribe with respect to such trust for such year
			 and before shall be responsible to ensure.</p>
<a id="H7B78980E3F504066A1E997902086FBF8"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(b) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Effective
			 date</span>.The amendment made by this section shall apply to taxable
			 years beginning after the date of the enactment of this Act.</p>
<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHang"><a href="#H9D351F98A5024AFDACBF5E39E7D6133B" id="toc-H9D351F98A5024AFDACBF5E39E7D6133B"><div class="lbexHangWithMargin">
<span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"><a id="H9D351F98A5024AFDACBF5E39E7D6133B"></a>SEC. 405.</span><span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"> <span class="lbexAllcap">Minimum penalty with
			 respect to failure to report on certain foreign trusts</span>.</span>
</div></a></p>
<a id="HDDA10D5DAF8E48F1AC0424931F80B77B"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(a) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">In
			 general</span>.Subsection (a) of
			 section 6677 is amended<a id="H5091E9AA94824AECB9E2AEA26F23086F"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) by inserting
			 the greater of $10,000 or before 35 percent,
			 and</p></p><a id="HA677437FD46E44EF9F0AD7E80B716969"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) by striking the
			 last sentence and inserting the following: At such time as the gross
			 reportable amount with respect to any failure can be determined by the
			 Secretary, any subsequent penalty imposed under this subsection with respect to
			 such failure shall be reduced as necessary to assure that the aggregate amount
			 of such penalties do not exceed the gross reportable amount (and to the extent
			 that such aggregate amount already exceeds the gross reportable amount the
			 Secretary shall refund such excess to the taxpayer).</p></p></p>
<a id="H463D66BB43D34C058851F0BEE22484D3"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(b) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Effective
			 date</span>.The amendments made by this section shall apply to notices
			 and returns required to be filed after December 31, 2009.</p>
<a id="H6AE826263F084DAB86EE701AE06EA42B"></a><p><div style="text-align:center"><a href="#H6AE826263F084DAB86EE701AE06EA42B" id="toc-H6AE826263F084DAB86EE701AE06EA42B"><span class="lbexTitleLevelOLC">TITLE V</span><span class="lbexTitleLevelOLC"><span style="text-align:center"></span><span class="lbexAllcap">Dividend
			 equivalent payments received by foreign persons treated as dividends</span></span></a></div></p>
<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexHang"><a href="#H464E12F1029A4E1385170C9507A3F5BF" id="toc-H464E12F1029A4E1385170C9507A3F5BF"><div class="lbexHangWithMargin">
<span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"><a id="H464E12F1029A4E1385170C9507A3F5BF"></a>SEC. 501.</span><span class=" lbexSectionlevelOLC"> <span class="lbexAllcap">Dividend equivalent
			 payments received by foreign persons treated as dividends</span>.</span>
</div></a></p>
<a id="H19506A4DBC2441FA91111B2FD8A460F6"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(a) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">In
			 general</span>.Section 871 is amended by redesignating subsection (l) as
			 subsection (m) and by inserting after subsection (k) the following new
			 subsection:<p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent"><a id="HF5188E9C05CB4C71B785BAA6B2CA7156"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentSubsection"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(l) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Treatment of
				dividend equivalent payments</span>.<a id="HC4FA8CB4797D413981DA90FB2338543D"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(1) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">I</span><span class="lbexSmallText">N
				GENERAL</span>.For purposes of this
				section, sections 881 and 4948(a), and chapters 3 and 4, a dividend equivalent
				shall be treated as a dividend from sources within the United States.</p></p><a id="H27ED2974F62E4B1B8C9445660363A6EB"></a><p style="margin-left: 0em;"><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndentParagraph">(2) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">D</span><span class="lbexSmallText">IVIDEND
				EQUIVALENT</span>.For purposes of this subsection<a id="HEE003A6277FC4548BE331AF2E319DDFB"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(A) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">I</span><span class="lbexSmallText">N
				GENERAL</span>.The term dividend equivalent means<a id="HD00E553CE0084CBA801AD068AB4CAC25"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(i) any payment made pursuant to a notional
				principal contract that (directly or indirectly) is contingent upon, or
				determined by reference to, the payment of a dividend from sources within the
				United States, and</p></p><a id="H3AFFE796F37045C895A9D1AC1A11E454"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(ii) any other payment determined by the
				Secretary to be substantially similar to a payment described in clause
				(i).</p></p></p></p><a id="H637AE0051FD549C0A2A231026DB5232B"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(B) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">E</span><span class="lbexSmallText">XCEPTIONS</span>.Such
				term does not include any payment pursuant to any contract or other arrangement
				which the Secretary determines does not have the potential for tax avoidance.
				In making such determination, the Secretary may take into account the following
				factors with respect to such contract or arrangement:<a id="H809BA3220DD4482BAD1CE1CB2AB436E9"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(i) The term (including provisions for early
				terminations and offsetting financial contracts).</p></p><a id="HE69BE8E4466D4D84AEA7D386553F5DE2"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(ii) The amount of each partys investment and
				the amounts of any collateral posted.</p></p><a id="H6433B62684D048CE835A54B34D2C4490"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(iii) Whether the
				price of the equity used to measure the parties entitlements or obligations is
				based on an objectively observable price.</p></p><a id="H12D656B8240E41CCB077B0283D46ED1E"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(iv) Whether either party sells (directly or
				indirectly) to the other party the security giving rise to dividends from
				sources within the United States.</p></p><a id="H25E0B34DC19542668C1FFE17C507031B"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(v) Whether there are terms that address the
				hedge position of either party or other conditions which would compel either
				party to hold or acquire the security giving rise to dividends from sources
				within the United States.</p></p><a id="H5C1F5045F33D4322A8EEC34894258619"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentClause">(vi) Such other
				factors as the Secretary determines appropriate.</p></p></p></p><a id="H02BD855A3D5C4F2BB2B390E093B7F7F5"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(C) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">P</span><span class="lbexSmallText">AYMENTS
				DETERMINED ON GROSS BASIS</span>.The
				term payment includes any gross amount which is used in
				computing any net amount which is transferred to or from the taxpayer.</p></p><a id="HEFA220F0A2294297B71106564C2A608A"></a><p style="margin-left: -2em;"><p class="lbexIndentSubpar">(D) <span style="font-size:110%; text-transform: capitalize ">C</span><span class="lbexSmallText">OORDINATION
				WITH CHAPTERS 3 AND 4</span>.For purposes of chapters 3 and 4, each
				person that is a party to any contract or other arrangement that provides for
				the payment of a dividend equivalent shall be treated as having control of such
				payment..</p></p></p></p></p></p></p></p>
<a id="H6AC45FC40EC84B5DBDBA9A8BE971B68E"></a><p style="text-align:left" class="lbexIndent">(b) <span class="lbexSectionLevelOLCnuclear">Effective
			 date</span>.The amendments made by this section shall apply to payments
			 made on or after the date that is 90 days after the date of the enactment of
			 this Act.</p>
</div>

    <script type="text/javascript">
    $(function () {
        var scroll_timer,
            displayed = false,
            $message = $('.top-link a').hide(),
            $window = $(window),
            top = $(document.body).children(0).position().top;

        $("#sticky-back-to-top").click(function(event){
            $window.scrollTop(0);
            event.preventDefault();
            return false;
        });

        $window.scroll(function () {
            window.clearTimeout(scroll_timer);
            scroll_timer = window.setTimeout(function () {
                if($window.scrollTop() <= top){
                    displayed = false;
                    $message.fadeOut(800);
                }else if(displayed == false){
                    displayed = true;
                    $message.stop(true, true).show().click(function () { $message.fadeOut(800); });
                }
            }, 100);
        });
    });
    </script>

    $(document).ready(function(){
        var h = window.location.hash,
            scrollTo = 0;

        if (h) {
            if ($(h).offset() !== undefined) {
                scrollTo = $(h).offset().top;
            }
        }

        if (scrollTo > 0) {
            $('html, body').stop().animate({ scrollTop : scrollTo + "px"}, 0);
        }

        $('body').congress_LAC({ checkUrl: '/lac/check' });
    });
